1476<div>

1477<h2>

1478Laminate Flooring</h2>

1479

1480<p>

1481Laminate is a flexible flooring style given its durability and the variety of styles it comes in. It can easily mimic the look of stone or wood. The core of laminate is made from wood clippings, melamine resin, and more to create a solid core. Real wood or stone is photographed and printed to create a photo layer. The photo layer is placed on the core, then a transparent wear layer is fused on top for protection. This process allows laminate flooring to withstand daily wear and tear. Browse our collection of laminate flooring, available in a selection of sizes, colors, textures, and more!&nbsp;</p>

This process allows laminate flooring to withstand daily wear and tear.
